<review>My car broke down the other night at the end of the Florin Road freeway off-ramp, which is a VERY unsafe place for a car to be parked...I was able to get it out of the exit lane & on to the shoulder a little, but it was not in a safe place, and I was really worried somebody might hit it when exiting the freeway because it was a wet night and my hazard lights were not very noticeable so I did not want to stay in my vehicle while I waited for the tow truck that I had already called.  The awesome guy at Enforcement Tow saw me and my car on the side of the road and even though he was already towing a vehicle, pulled over to see if I needed any help.  He was really concerned about my safety, and offered to stay there with me while I waited for my tow truck and turned on the lights on his truck so that other vehicles could now easily see the hazard (my sad broken Toyota) ahead.  He was obviously on his way someplace, and his walkie talkie kept going off but he hung out until my tow truck arrived and he knew my car and I were safe and on our way.  Before he had arrived I was nervously standing on the side of the road by myself in the dark, worrying about creepy people trying to lure me in to their cars (which had already happened twice in the 10 minutes I had been waiting).  I really appreciated what the tow guy did, and I just wanted to let people know that Enforcement Tow isn't all about just towing vehicles parked where they are not supposed to be.  They didn't make any money by staying parked on the side of the road with me until my help arrived, but they made my bad night a lot better and safer and I really appreciated that. <Text>This place hits home for me! I grew up in the country side where you wake up every morning & walk down the streets to say hello to the whole town! A regular customer who probably live down the street enters & says hello to everyone especially all the ladies & topped it off with a hug. I felt like the only stranger in the room but it felt good because this spot is the true definition of a Ma & Pa joint!

I love the unique coffee mugs that they serve with coffee. Every mug is different & has its own design. It's like opening my cabinet at home! I thought it was cute that I landed a Christmas mug in the middle of summer!

I ordered the hash browns. It was truly perfection. Crispy on the outside & soft but yet firm in the inside. The best part was that it's not greasy.

I had the Omelette which was made up of fresh ingredients & the eggs was cooked into a light & fluffy texture. I know eggs & if you overcook eggs; it becomes hard & gives off a slight egg odor.<//Text>< Rating>
